# Test Report

Time: 2024-04-14 11:24:28.248869

### Base Program

```py
def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans
```

## Test Case 1

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, curr=None, remaining_fuel=None, memo=None):
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
     
    if curr is None:
        curr = start
        remaining_fuel = fuel

    if remaining_fuel < 0:
        return 0

    if (curr, remaining_fuel) in memo:
        return memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)]

    ans = 1 if curr == finish else 0
    for next in range(len(locations)):
        if next != curr:
            ans += count_routes(locations, start, finish, fuel, next, remaining_fuel - abs(locations[curr] - locations[next]), memo)
            ans %= 1000000007

    memo[(curr, remaining_fuel)] = ans
    return ans


```
